Introduction

Base URL: https://api.nextenvios.cl

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

To authenticate requests, include an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Auth management

APIs for managing auth

Register

Registra un Usuario. Si todo esta bien, retorna una respuesta 200 OK

Si no retorna un error 422 que indica que hay errores en el body.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/register" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"slsufotassanekqz\",
    \"name2\": \"qzcgvuehd\",
    \"last_name\": \"gbirlajtjckqudangimzghj\",
    \"last_name2\": \"ab\",
    \"rut\": \"vpoiybrd\",
    \"email\": \"ratke.kenneth@example.org\",
    \"password\": \"%0@WXo[\",
    \"password_confirmation\": \"password123\",
    \"phone\": \"rvihkkyrsezltyfywjl\",
    \"gender\": \"other\",
    \"provider_id\": \"ratione\",
    \"company_id\": \"magni\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/register"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "slsufotassanekqz",
    "name2": "qzcgvuehd",
    "last_name": "gbirlajtjckqudangimzghj",
    "last_name2": "ab",
    "rut": "vpoiybrd",
    "email": "ratke.kenneth@example.org",
    "password": "%0@WXo[",
    "password_confirmation": "password123",
    "phone": "rvihkkyrsezltyfywjl",
    "gender": "other",
    "provider_id": "ratione",
    "company_id": "magni"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (422, El body tiene errores.):


{
    "message": "The password field confirmation does not match. (and 3 more errors)",
    "errors": {
        "password": [
            "The password field confirmation does not match."
        ],
        "password_confirmation": [
            "The password confirmation field is required."
        ],
        "provider_id": [
            "The selected provider id is invalid."
        ],
        "company_id": [
            "The selected company id is invalid."
        ]
    }
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/auth/register

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

name   string   

Must not be greater than 100 characters. Example: slsufotassanekqz

name2   string  optional  

Must not be greater than 100 characters. Example: qzcgvuehd

last_name   string   

Must not be greater than 100 characters. Example: gbirlajtjckqudangimzghj

last_name2   string  optional  

Must not be greater than 100 characters. Example: ab

rut   string   

Must not be greater than 20 characters. Example: vpoiybrd

email   string   

Must be a valid email address. Must not be greater than 40 characters. Example: ratke.kenneth@example.org

password   string   

Must be at least 6 characters. Example: %0@WXo[

password_confirmation   string  optional  

The confirmed password. Example: password123

phone   string   

Must not be greater than 20 characters. Example: rvihkkyrsezltyfywjl

gender   string   

Example: other

Must be one of:
  • male
  • female
  • other
provider_id   string  optional  

Example: ratione

company_id   string  optional  

Example: magni

Response

Response Fields

message      

Mensaje de error

errors      

Informacion detallada sobre los errores

Login

Check that the service is up. If everything is okay, you'll get a 200 OK response.

Otherwise, the request will fail with a 400 error, and a response listing the failed services.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"quis\",
    \"password\": \"voluptas\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "quis",
    "password": "voluptas"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (400, Service is unhealthy):


{
    "status": "down",
    "services": {
        "database": "up",
        "redis": "down"
    }
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/auth/login

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

email   string   

Example: quis

password   string   

Example: voluptas

Response

Response Fields

status      

The status of this API (up or down).

services      

Map of each downstream service and their status (up or down).

POST api/auth/forgot-password

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/forgot-password" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"thelma.ohara@example.net\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/forgot-password"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "thelma.ohara@example.net"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Example: thelma.ohara@example.net

POST api/auth/reset-password

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/reset-password" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"token\": \"non\",
    \"email\": \"steuber.caleigh@example.com\",
    \"password\": \"POjV,$.p|>sv:fO@>O\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/auth/reset-password"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "token": "non",
    "email": "steuber.caleigh@example.com",
    "password": "POjV,$.p|>sv:fO@>O"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/auth/reset-password

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

token   string   

Example: non

email   string   

Must be a valid email address. Example: steuber.caleigh@example.com

password   string   

Must be at least 6 characters. Example: POjV,$.p|>sv:fO@>O

City management

APIs for managing City

Display a listing of the resource.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/cities" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"region_id\": \"26853dbd-2133-352e-ab37-ce97baa78bc6\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/cities"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "region_id": "26853dbd-2133-352e-ab37-ce97baa78bc6"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

    --form "business_name=rem"\
    --form "rut=natus"\
    --form "address=est"\
    --form "phone=placeat"\
    --form "mobile=deleniti"\
    --form "city_id=omnis"\
    --form "file=@/tmp/phpdXJ1ml"

    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/companies"
);

};

body.append('mobile', 'deleniti');
body.append('city_id', 'omnis');

    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

'provider_id' => 'nullable|string|exists:providers,id',. Example: et

city_id   string[]  optional  

Display a listing of the resource.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/delivery-packs" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"date\": \"2024-07-11T15:03:43\",
    \"company_id\": \"animi\",
    \"city_id\": [
        \"molestiae\"
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/delivery-packs"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "date": "2024-07-11T15:03:43",
    "company_id": "animi",
    "city_id": [
        "molestiae"
    ]
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/providers" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "name=qbbo"\
    --form "business_name=gvctkmmzgvlkkuzhnth"\
    --form "rut=m"\
    --form "address=vero"\
    --form "phone=sctv"\
    --form "mobile=gzthydasf"\
    --form "tracking_link=temporibus"\
    --form "city_id=sit"\
    --form "company_id=quis"\
    --form "file=@/tmp/phpF0zMlv" 
const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/providers"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('name', 'qbbo');
body.append('business_name', 'gvctkmmzgvlkkuzhnth');
body.append('rut', 'm');
body.append('address', 'vero');
body.append('phone', 'sctv');
body.append('mobile', 'gzthydasf');
body.append('tracking_link', 'temporibus');
body.append('city_id', 'sit');
body.append('company_id', 'quis');
body.append('file', document.querySelector('input[name="file"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

    \"new_users\": [

    ],
    \"remove_users\": [
        \"porro\"
    ]
}"

);

};

    ],
    "remove_users": [
        "porro"
    ]
};

Update user profile

requires authentication

Updates the authenticated user's profile information.

Example request:
curl --request PUT \
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/users" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"John\",
    \"name2\": \"Alex\",
    \"last_name\": \"Doe\",
    \"last_name2\": \"Smith\",
    \"rut\": \"mquuzfwqqmkavhwuz\",
    \"gender\": \"male\",
    \"phone\": \"+1234567890\",
    \"email\": \"john.doe@example.com\",
    \"current_password\": \"pmtwvdgbixzopuxlwhultwnlgritekcpdebtyvubzhikv\",
    \"password\": \"password123\",
    \"password_confirmation\": \"password123\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.nextenvios.cl/api/users"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "John",
    "name2": "Alex",
    "last_name": "Doe",
    "last_name2": "Smith",
    "rut": "mquuzfwqqmkavhwuz",
    "gender": "male",
    "phone": "+1234567890",
    "email": "john.doe@example.com",
    "current_password": "pmtwvdgbixzopuxlwhultwnlgritekcpdebtyvubzhikv",
    "password": "password123",
    "password_confirmation": "password123"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
    "id": "9c7c5310-aeec-413c-9b4b-d98a234be4fd",
    "name": "John",
    "last_name": "Doe",
    "name2": "Alex",
    "last_name2": "Smith",
    "email": "john.doe@example.com",
    "phone": "+1234567890",
    "gender": "male",
    "is_active": true,
    "created_at": "2024-07-10T16:13:40.000000Z",
    "updated_at": "2024-07-10T16:13:40.000000Z"
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

PUT api/users

Headers

Authorization      

Example: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

name   string   

The first name of the user. Example: John

name2   string  optional  

The second first name of the user. Example: Alex

last_name   string   

The last name of the user. Example: Doe

last_name2   string  optional  

The second last name of the user. Example: Smith

rut   string  optional  

Must not be greater than 20 characters. Example: mquuzfwqqmkavhwuz

gender   string  optional  

The gender of the user. Must be one of 'male', 'female', 'other'. Example: male

phone   string  optional  

The phone number of the user. Example: +1234567890

email   string   

The email of the user. Example: john.doe@example.com

current_password   string  optional  

Must be at least 6 characters. Example: pmtwvdgbixzopuxlwhultwnlgritekcpdebtyvubzhikv

password   string   

The new password for the user. Example: password123

password_confirmation   string   

The password confirmation for the user. Example: password123
